book i
man first disobedi fruit
forbidden tree whose mortal tast
brought death into world all our woe
loss eden till on greater man
restor us regain bliss seat
sing heav’nly muse secret top
oreb or sinai didst inspir
shepherd who first taught chosen seed
begin how heav’ns earth
rose out chao or if sion hill
delight thee more siloa’s brook flow’d
fast oracl god i thenc
ok thy aid my adventr song
no middl flight intend soar
ov th’ aonian mount while pursu
thing unattempt yet prose or rhime
d chiefli thou o spirit dost prefer
or all templ th’ upright heart pure
truct me thou know’st thou first
present mighti wing outspread
dovelik satst brood vast abyss
d mad’st pregnant what me dark
illumin what low rais support
highth thi great argument
i mai assert th’ etern provid
d justifi way god men
sai first heav’n hide noth thy view
nor deep tract hell sai first what caus
mov’d our grand parent happi state
favour’d heav’n so highli fall off
r creator transgress hi 
restraint lord world besid
who first seduc’d them fowl revolt
th’ infern serpent whose guil
stird up envi reveng deceiv’d
mother mankind what time hi pride
had cast him out heav’n all hi host
rebel angel whose aid aspir
set himself glori abov hi peer
trust have equal’d most high
if oppos’d ambiti aim
ainst throne monarchi god
rais’d impiou war heav’n battel proud
vain attempt  him almighti power
hurld headlong flame th’ ether skie
hideou ruin combust down
bottomless perdit there dwell
adamantin chain penal fire
who durst defi th’ omnipot arm
nine time space measur dai night
mortal men hi horrid crew
lai vanquisht rowl fieri gulf
confound though immort but hi doom
reserv’d him more wrath now thought
both lost happi last pain
ment him round throw hi bale ey
witness’d huge afflict dismai
mixt obdur pride stedfast hate
onc far angel kenn view
dismal situat wast wild
dungeon horribl all side round
on great furnac flam’d yet those flame
no light but rather dark visibl
serv’d onli discov sight woe
region sorrow dole shade where peac
d rest can never dwell hope never come
come all but tortur without end
still urg fieri delug fed
everburn sulphur unconsum’d
such place etern justic had prepar’d
those rebelli here their prison ordain’d
utter dark their portion set
far remov’d god light heav’n
center thrice th’ utmost pole
o how unlik place whenc thei fell
e companion hi fall o’rewhelm’d
flood whirlwind tempestu fire
soon discern weltr hi side
next himself power next crime
long after known palestin nam’d
lzebub  whom th’ archenemi
d thenc heav’n call’d satan bold word
break horrid silenc thu began
if thou beest but o how fall’n how chang’d
him who happi realm light
cloth’d transcend brightn didst outshin
myriad though bright if whom mutual leagu
unit thought counsel equal hope
d hazard gloriou enterpr
joynd me onc now miseri hath joynd
equal ruin into what pit thou seest
what highth fal’n so much stronger provd
hi thunder till then who knew
forc those dire arm yet not those
nor what potent victor hi rage
can els inflict do i repent or chang
though chang’d outward lustr fixt mind
d high disdain senc injur’d merit
mightiest rais’d me contend
d fierc content brought along
umer forc spirit arm’d
durst dislik hi reign me prefer
hi utmost power advers power oppos’d
dubiou battel plain heav’n
d shook hi throne  what though field lost
l not lost unconquer 
d studi reveng immort hate
d courag never submit or yield
d what els not overcom
glori never shall hi wrath or might
extort me  bow sue grace
suppliant knee deifi hi power
who terrour thi arm so late
doubt hi empir low inde
ignomini shame beneath
thi downfal sinc fate strength god
d thi empyr substanc cannot fail
sinc through experi thi great event
arm not wors foresight much advanc’t
we mai more success hope resolv
wage forc or guil etern warr
irreconcil our grand foe
who now triumph th’ excess joi
sole reign hold tyranni heav’n
so spake th’ apost angel though pain
vaunt aloud but rackt deep despar
d him thu answer’d soon hi bold compeer
o princ o chief mani throne power
led th’ imbattelld seraphim warr
under thy conduct dread deed
fearless endanger’d heav’ns perpetu king
d put proof hi high supremaci
whether upheld strength or chanc or fate
well i see rue dire event
sad overthrow foul defeat
hath lost us heav’n all thi mighti host
horribl destruct laid thu low
far god heav’nly essenc
can perish mind spirit remain
incibl vigour soon return
though all our glori extinct happi state
e swallow’d up endless miseri
but what if our conquerour whom i now
forc believ almighti sinc no less
such could hav orepow’rd such forc our
have left us thi our spirit strength intir
strongli suffer support our pain
we mai so suffic hi veng ir
or do him mightier servic hi thrall
right warr what e’re hi busi 
e heart hell work fire
or do hi errand gloomi deep
what can then avail though yet we feel
strength undiminisht or etern be
undergo etern punish
whereto speedi word th’ archfiend reply’d
fall’n cherub weak miser
do or suffer but thi sure
do ought good never our task
but ever do ill our sole delight
be contrari hi high 
whom we resist  if then hi provid
out our evil seek bring forth good
our labour must pervert end
d out good still find mean evil
which oft time mai succe so perhap
shall griev him if i fail not disturb
hi inmost counsel their destind aim
but see angri victor hath recall’d
hi minist vengeanc pursuit
back gate heav’n sulphur hail
shot after us storm oreblown hath laid
fieri surg precipic
heav’n receiv’d us fall thunder
wing’d red lightn impetu rage
perhap hath spent hi shaft ceas now
bellow through vast boundless deep
let us not slip th’ occas whether scorn
or satiat furi yield our foe
seest thou yon dreari plain forlorn wild
seat desol voyd light
save what glimmer these livid flame
cast pale dread  thither let us tend
toss these fieri wave
e rest if ani rest can harbour there
d reassembl our afflict power
consult how we mai henceforth most offend
our enemi our own loss how repair
how overcom thi dire calam
what reinforc we mai gain hope
if not what resolut despar
thu satan talk hi neerest mate
head uplift abov wave ey
sparkl blaz’d hi other part besid
prone flood extend long larg
lai float mani rood bulk huge
whom fabl name monstrou size
titanian or earthborn warr’d jove
briario or typhon whom den
ancient tarsu held or seabeast
leviathan which god all hi work
creat hugest swim th’ ocean stream
him hapli slumbr norwai foam
pilot some small nightfounder’d skiff
deem some island oft seamen tell
fix anchor hi skali rind
moor hi side under lee while night
est sea wish morn delay
so stretcht out huge length archfiend lai
chain’d burn lake nor ever thenc
had ris’n or heav’d hi head but 
d high permiss allrul heaven
left him larg hi own dark design
reiter crime might
p himself damnat while sought
evil other enrag’d might see
how all hi malic serv’d but bring forth
init good grace merci shewn
man him seduc’t but himself
trebl confus wrath vengeanc pour’d
hwith upright rear off pool
hi mighti statur each hand flame
drivn backward slope their point spire  rowld
billow leav i’th’ midst horrid vale
expand wing stear hi flight
incumb duski air
felt unusu weight till dry land
light if land ever burn’d
solid lake liquid fire
d such appear’d hue when forc
subterranean wind transport hill
n peloru or shatter’d side
thundr aetna whose combust
d fewel’d entral thenc conceiv fire
sublim’d miner furi aid wind
d leav sing bottom all involv’d
stench smoak such rest found sole
unblest feet  him follow hi next mate
both glori have scap’t stygian flood
god their own recover’d strength
not suffer supern power
thi region thi soil clime
said then lost arch angel thi seat
we must chang heav’n thi mourn gloom
celesti light  so sinc hee
who now sovran can dispos bid
what shall right fardest him best
whom reason hath equald forc hath made supream
ov hi equal  farewel happi field
where joi ever dwell hail horrour hail
ernal world thou profoundest hell
receiv thy new possessor on who bring
mind not chang’d place or time
mind own place self
can make heav’n hell hell heav’n
what matter where if i still same
d what i should all but less then hee
whom thunder hath made greater  here least
we shall free th’ almighti hath not built
e hi envi not drive us henc
e we mai reign secur my choyc
reign worth ambit though hell
ter reign hell then serv heav’n
but wherefor let we then our faith friend
th’ associ copartn our loss
lye thu astonisht th’ oblivi pool
d call them not share us their part
thi unhappi mansion or onc more
ralli arm try what mai yet
regaind heav’n or what more lost hell
so satan spake him beelzebub
thu answer’d  leader those armi bright
which but th’ omnipot none could have foyld
if onc thei hear voyc their liveliest pledg
hope fear danger heard so oft
worst extream peril edg
battel when rag’d all assault
r surest signal thei soon resum
new courag reviv though now thei lye
grovel prostrat yon lake fire
we erewhil astound amaz’d
no wonder fall’n such pernici highth
scarc had ceas’t when superiour fiend
move toward shore hi ponder shield
ether temper massi larg round
him cast broad circumfer
hung hi shoulder like moon whose orb
through optic glass tuscan artist view
ev’ning top fesol
or valdarno descri new land
river or mountain her spotti globe
hi spear equal which tallest pine
n norwegian hill mast
some great ammir but wand
walkt support uneasi step
over burn marl not like those step
heaven azur torrid clime
smote him sore besid vault fire
nathless so endur’d till beach
inflam sea stood call’d
hi legion angel form who lai intrans’t
thick autumn leav strow brook
vallombrosa where th’ etrurian shade
high overarch’t imbowr or scatterd sedg
loat when fierc wind orion arm’d
hath vext redsea coast whose wave orethrew
busiri hi memphian chivalri
vvhile perfidi hatr thei pursu’d
sojourn goshen who beheld
safe shore their float carkas
d broken chariot wheel so thick bestrown
ject lost lai these cover flood
under amaz their hideou chang
call’d so loud all hollow deep
hell resound  princ potent
warrier flowr heav’n onc your now lost
if such astonish thi can siez
etern spirit or have ye chos’n thi place
ter toyl battel repos
your weari vertu eas you find
slumber here vale heav’n
or thi abject postur have ye sworn
ador conquerour who now behold
cherub seraph rowl flood
scatter’d arm ensign till anon
hi swift pursuer heav’n gate discern
th’ advantag descend tread us down
thu droop or link thunderbolt
transfix us bottom thi gulf
ak aris or ever fall’n
heard abasht up thei sprung
upon wing when men wont watch
duti sleep found whom thei dread
rous bestir themselv er well awak
nor did thei not perceav evil plight
which thei or fierc pain not feel
yet their gener voyc thei soon obeyd
umer  when potent rod
amram son egypt evil dai
wav’d round coast up call’d pitchi cloud
locust warp eastern wind
or realm impiou pharoah hung
like night darken’d all land nile
so numberless those bad angel seen
hover wing under cope hell
’twixt upper nether surround fire
till signal giv’n th’ uplift spear
r great sultan wave direct
thir cours even ballanc down thei light
firm brimston fill all plain
multitud like which popul north
pour’d never her frozen loyn pass
rhene or danaw when her barbar son
came like delug south spread
eath gibraltar lybian sand
hwith everi squadron each band
head leader thither hast where stood
r great command godlik shape form
excel human princ digniti
d power earst heaven sat throne
though their name heav’nly record now
no memori blot out ras’d
thir rebellion book life
nor had thei yet among son ev
got them new name till wandr or earth
through god high suffer tryal man
falsiti lye greatest part
mankind thei corrupt forsak
god their creator th’ invis
glori him made them transform
imag brute adorn’d
gai religion full pomp gold
d devil ador deiti
thei known men variou name
d variou idol through heathen world
sai muse their name then known who first who last
rous’d slumber fieri couch
thir great emperor call next worth
came singli where stood bare strand
while promiscu croud stood yet aloof
chief those who pit hell
roam seek their prei earth durst fix
r seat long after next seat god
r altar hi altar god ador’d
nation round durst abid
jehovah thundr out sion thron’d
ween cherubim yea often plac’d
n hi sanctuari self their shrine
omin curs thing
hi holi rite solemn feast profan’d
d their dark durst affront hi light
first moloch horrid king besmear’d blood
human sacrific parent tear
though noys drum timbrel loud
r children cri unheard past through fire
hi grim idol  him ammonit
worshipt rabba her watri plain
argob basan stream
utmost arnon  nor content such
daciou neighbourhood wisest heart
solomon led fraud build
hi templ right against templ god
opprobri hill made hi grove
pleasant valli hinnom tophet thenc
d black gehenna call’d type hell
next chemo th’ obscen dread moab son
aroer nebo wild
southmost abarim hesebon
d heronaim seon realm beyond
flowri dale sibma clad vine
d eleal th’ asphaltick pool
peor hi other name when entic’d
ael sittim their march nile
do him wanton rite which cost them woe
yet thenc hi lust orgi enlarg’d
even hill scandal grove
moloch homicid lust hard hate
till good josiah drove them thenc hell
these came thei who bordr flood
old euphrat brook part
egypt syrian ground had gener name
baalim ashtaroth those male
e feminin  spirit when thei pleas
can either sex assum or both so soft
d uncompound their essenc pure
not ti’d or manacl’d joynt or limb
nor found brittl strength bone
like cumbrou flesh but what shape thei choos
dilat or condens’t bright or obscur
can execut their aeri purpos
d work love or enmiti fulfil
those race israel oft forsook
r live strength unfrequ left
hi righteou altar bow lowli down
bestial god which their head low
bow’d down battel sunk befor spear
despic foe  these troop
came astoreth whom phoenician call’d
tart queen heav’n crescent horn
whose bright imag nightli moon
sidonian virgin paid their vow song
sion also not unsung where stood
templ th’ offens mountain built
uxori king whose heart though larg
uil’d fair idolatress fell
idol foul thammuz came next behind
whose annual wound lebanon allur’d
syrian damsel lament hi fate
amor ditty all summer dai
while smooth adoni hi nativ rock
ran purpl sea suppos’d blood
thammuz yearli wound lovetal
ect sion daughter like heat
whose wanton passion sacr porch
ezekiel saw when vision led
hi ey survay’d dark idolatri
alien judah  next came on
who mourn’d earnest when captiv ark
maim’d hi brute imag head hand lopt off
hi own templ grunsel edg
where fell flat sham’d hi worship
dagon hi name sea monster upward man
d downward fish yet had hi templ high
rear’d azotu dread through coast
palestin gath ascalon
d accaron gaza’s frontier bound
him follow’d rimmon whose delight seat
fair damscu fertil bank
abbana pharphar lucid stream
also against hous god bold
leper onc lost gain’d king
az hi sottish conquerour whom drew
god altar disparag displac
syrian mode whereon burn
hi odiou offr ador god
whom had vanquisht after these appear’d
crew who under name old renown
osiri isi oru their train
monstrou shape sorceri abus’d
fanat egypt her priest seek
thir wandr god disguis’d brutish form
rather then human  nor did israel scape
th’ infect when their borrow’d gold compos’d
calf oreb rebel king
doubl’d sin bethel dan
lik’ning hi maker graze ox
jehovah who on night when pass’d
egypt march equal’d on stroke
both her first born all her bleat god
ial came last then whom spirit more lewd
fell not heaven or more gross love
vice self him no templ stood
or altar smoak’d yet who more oft then hee
templ altar when priest
turn atheist did ely’s son who fill’d
lust violenc hous god
court palac also reign
d luxuri citi where noys
riot ascend abov thir loftiest towr
d injuri outrag when night
darken street then wander forth son
belial flown insol wine
wit street sodom night
gibeah when hospit dore
yield thir matron prevent wors rape
e prime order might
rest long tell though far renown’d
th’ ionian god javan issu held
god yet confest later then heav’n earth
thir boast parent titan heav’ns first born
hi enorm brood birthright seis’d
younger saturn mightier jove
hi own rhea’s son like measur found
so jove usurp reign’d these first creet
d ida known thenc snowi top
cold olympu rul’d middl air
thir highest heav’n or delphian cliff
or dodona through all bound
doric land or who saturn old
fled over adria th’ hesperian field
d or celtic roam’d utmost isl
l these more came flock but look
down cast damp yet such wherein appear’d
obscur som glimp joi have found thir chief
not despair have found themselv not lost
loss self which hi count’nanc cast
like doubt hue but hi wont pride
soon recollect high word bore
semblanc worth not substanc gentli rais’d
r faint courag dispel’d their fear
strait command warlik sound
trumpet loud clarion upreard
hi mighti standard proud honour claim’d

who forthwith glitter staff unfurld
th’ imperi ensign which full high advanc’t
shon like meteor stream wind
gemm golden lustr rich imblaz’d
seraph arm trophi all while
sonor mettal blow martial sound
which univers host upsent
shout tore hell concav beyond
fright reign chao old night
l moment through gloom seen
ten thousand banner rise into air
orient colour wave them rose
est huge spear throng helm
pear’d serri shield thick arrai
depth immeasur anon thei move
perfect phalanx dorian mood
flute soft record such rais’d
highth noblest temper hero’s old
ming battel stead rage
deliber valour breath’d firm unmov’d
dread death flight or foul retreat
nor want power mitig swage
solemn touch troubl’d thought chase
guish doubt fear sorrow pain
mortal or immort mind  thu thei
breath unit forc fix thought
mov’d silenc soft pipe charm’d
thir pain step o’re burnt soyl now
vanc’t view thei stand horrid front
dread length dazl arm guis
warrier old order’d spear shield
ait what command thir mighti chief
had impos through arm file
dart hi experienc’t ey soon travers
whole battalion view thir order due
thir visag statur god
thir number last summ  now hi heart
distend pride hardn hi strength
glori never sinc creat man
met such imbodi forc nam’d these
could merit more then small infantri
warr’d crane though all giant brood
phlegra th’ heroic race joyn’d
fought theb’s ilium each side
mixt auxiliar god what resound
fabl or romanc uther son
irt british armor knight
d all who sinc baptiz’d or infidel
joust aspramont or montalban
damasco or marocco or trebisond
or whom biserta sent afric shore

fontarabbia  thu far these beyond
compar mortal prowess yet observ’d
thir dread command abov rest
shape gestur proudli emin
stood like towr hi form had yet not lost
l her origin bright nor appear’d
less then arch angel ruind th’ excess
glori obscur’d when sun new ris’n
look through horizont misti air
shorn hi beam or behind moon
dim eclip disastr twilight shed
half nation fear chang
perplex monarch  dark’n’d so yet shon
ov them all th’ arch angel but hi face
deep scar thunder had intrencht care
sat hi fade cheek but under brow
dauntless courag consider pride
wait reveng cruel hi ey but cast
sign remors passion behold
fellow hi crime follow rather
far other onc beheld bliss condemn’d
ever now have their lot pain
million spirit hi fault amerc’t
heav’n etern splendor flung
hi revolt yet faithful how thei stood
thir glori witherd  when heaven fire
hath scath’d forrest oak or mountain pine
sing top their state growth though bare
stand blast heath  now prepar’d
speak whereat their doubl’d rank thei bend
wing wing half enclos him round
all hi peer attent held them mute
thrice assayd thrice spite scorn
tear such angel weep burst forth last
word interwov sigh found out their wai
o myriad immort spirit o power
matchless but th’ almighti strife
not inglori though th’ event dire
thi place testifi thi dire chang
hate utter but what power mind
see or presag depth
knowledg past or present could have fear’d
how such unit forc god how such
stood like these could ever know repuls
who can yet beleev though after loss
all these puissant legion whose exil
hath empti heav’n shall fail reascend
selfrais’d repossess their nativ seat
me wit all host heav’n
if counsel differ or danger shun’d
me have lost our hope  but who reign
monarch heav’n till then on secur
sat hi throne upheld old reput
consent or custom hi regal state
put forth full but still hi strength conceal’d
which tempt our attempt wrought our fall
ceforth hi might we know know our own
so not either provok or dread
new warr provok’t our better part remain
work close design fraud or guil
what forc effect not no less
length us mai find who overcom
e hath overcom but half hi foe
space mai produc new world whereof so rife
e went fame heav’n er long
end creat therein plant
gener whom hi choic regard
should favour equal son heaven
thither if but prie shall perhap
our first erupt thither or elsewher
thi infern pit shall never hold
caelesti spirit bondag nor th’ abyss
long under dark cover  but these thought
full counsel must matur peac despaird
who can think submiss  warr then warr
open or understood must resolv’d
spake confirm hi word outflew
million flame sword drawn thigh
mighti cherubim sudden blaze

hi womb hid metal or
work sulphur  thither wing’d speed
numer brigad hasten’d  when band
pioner spade pickax arm’d
run royal camp trench field
or cast rampart  mammon led them 
mammon least erect spirit fell
v’n ev’n heav’n hi look  thought
alwai downward bent admir more
rich heav’ns pavement trod’n gold
aught divin or holi els enjoy’d

d strength art easili outdon
spirit reprob hour
what ag thei incess toyl
d hand innumer scarc perform

variou mould boyl cell

dulcet symphoni voic sweet

d sat princ whom suprem king

each hi herarchi order bright

ancient greec ausonian land

d porch wide but chief spaciou hall
